attorneys, and court staff providing similar support may be expected, should not be discouraged, and is authorized provided it complies with legal and ethical standards.\n- Disclosure of AI use should not be required in a pleading.\n\n**Accountability and Review Requirements:**\n- Attorneys, judges, and self-represented litigants are accountable for their final work product.\n- All users must thoroughly review AI-generated content before submitting it in any court proceeding to ensure accuracy and compliance with legal and ethical obligations.\n\n**Ethical Standards:**\n- The Rules of Professional Conduct and the Code of Judicial Conduct apply fully to the use of AI technologies.\n\nNotably, the Illinois approach differs from many other jurisdictions by explicitly stating that
